* Taken many steps to remove the Redirector step of the Flashpoint framework, including:
 * All the Flash projectors have been modded to only talk to the server.
 * All the Shockwave projectors have been configured to only talk to the server.
 * Platforms that don't open Basilisk or projectors directly now parse through the Flashpoint Secure Player.
* Added the Flashpoint Secure Player to add redirectorless support for ActiveX, increase our ability to make and revert system changes, and add plugins we couldn't have before.
 * Added Clickteam Vitalize as a supported plugin.
 * Added Superscape's Viscape as a supported plugin.
 * Added Hypercosm as a supported plugin.
* The Logs tab now lists all files loaded from the server, replacing the Redirector's role in that.
* Fixed a handful of launcher bugs.
* Shockwave can now be opened in browser.
* Swapped out the Java implementation to OpenJDK.
* Updated the logo for HTML5 and ActiveX.
* Updated the readme to a proper PDF manual.
* Added several new playlists; Flash Food, Rage for the Ages and Toys to Enjoy.
* Added English version of Metele Al Ordenata (Bash the Computer).
* Added Neopets 'graveyard' versions of Evil Fuzzles from Beyond the Stars, Igloo Garage Sale: The Game, Usuki Frenzy!!!, Korbat's Lab, Dr. Sloth's Carnival of Terror, Maths Nightmare, Dubloon Disaster and 200m Peanut Dash.
* Added Slingo versions of Word Roundup Bingo, Word Roundup Frenzy and Picturiffic.
